    </ul></div> </div>

            <h2>UPDATE</h2>

            <h2>Science and Engineering</h2>
            <div class="s-grid"><article id="post-24439" class="content-item -caption post-24439 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-article category-exploration category-organization category-rocket-sciences category-science-and-engineering category-space-mission category-spacex tag-sn20 tag-spacex tag-starship tag-starship-prototype">

                <div><article id="post-24908" class="content-item -list post-24908 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-astronomy category-opinion category-planetary-science category-solar-system tag-asteroid tag-earth tag-meteor tag-solar-system tag-trojan-asteroid">
                <header class="entry-header">
                <h2 class="entry-title"><a href="https://spaceth.co/will-astroid-hit-earth-or-not/" rel="bookmark">สรุปดาวเคราะห์น้อย ดาวตก และอุกกาบาต รู้ไว้จะได้ไม่ต้องกลัว</a></h2> <div class="entry-meta">
                <span class="posted-on _heading"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="feather feather-clock"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><polyline points="12 6 12 12 16 14"></polyline></svg> <a href="https://spaceth.co/will-astroid-hit-earth-or-not/" rel="bookmark"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2021-06-25T09:48:20+07:00">June 25, 2021</time><time class="updated hide" datetime="2021-06-25T09:52:40+07:00">June 25, 2021</time></a></span> </div>

                <h2>Science and Engineering</h2>

                <a href="https://spaceth.co/starship-orbital-test/" title="Permalink to ทุกสิ่งที่ควรรู้ในการทดสอบยาน Starship เต็มรูปแบบ ขึ้นสู่วงโคจรภายในปีนี้" rel="bookmark">

                <h2>Content</h2>
                <div class="s-grid"><article id="post-24547" class="content-item -hero post-24547 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-article category-astronomy category-biotech-for-space category-feature category-mars-exploration category-nasa category-search-for-life category-solar-system category-space-mission tag-extraterrestrial tag-life tag-life-in-space tag-mars tag-mars-2020 tag-mars-exploration tag-mars-landing tag-mars-rover tag-mars-sample-return tag-nasa tag-perseverance tag-search-for-life">
